maxPerNamespace,\n\t\tnamespacePolicyCounts: make(map[string]int),\n\t}\n}\n\n// Run starts the controller and watches for CiliumNetworkPolicy events.\n// It updates the per-namespace policy counts as is an update of an existing policy in the same namespace, count stays the same\n\t// If this is a new policy, increment the count\n\t// We check the namespace to see if this is the first policy\n\tif c.namespacePolicyCounts[namespace] == 0 {\n\t\t// First policy in this namespace\n\t\tc.log.WithFields(logrus.Fields{\n\t\t\tlogfields.K8sNamespace: we've seen\n\t// For now, we'll just ensure the count is at least 1 when a policy exists\n\tif c.namespacePolicyCounts[namespace] == 0 {\n\t\tc.namespacePolicyCounts[namespace] = 1\n\t}\n}\n\n// handleDelete decrements the policy count when a CiliumNetworkPolicy is deleted.\nfunc (c *PolicyQuotaController) handleDelete(cnp *cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy) {\n\tnamespace := cnp.Namespace\n\tname := cnp.Name\n\n\tc.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer c.mu.Unlock()\n\n\tif count, ok := c.namespacePolicyCounts[namespace]; ok && count > 0 {\n\t\tcount--\n\t\tif count == 0 given namespace has exceeded its policy quota.\n// It returns an error if the quota is exceeded, nil otherwise.\nfunc (c *PolicyQuotaController) CheckQuota(namespace string) error {\n\t// If maxPerNamespace is 0, quota is unlimited\n\tif c.maxPerNamespace == 0 {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\n\tc.mu.RLock()\n\tcount := c.namespacePolicyCounts[namespace]\n\tc.mu.RUnlock()\n\n\tif count >= %d\",\n\t\t\tnamespace,\n\t\t\tcount,\n\t\t\tc.maxPerNamespace,\n\t\t)\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// GetNamespacePolicyCount returns the number of policies in the given namespace.\n// This is A value of 0 means unlimited.\nfunc NewPolicyQuotaController(\n\tlog logrus.FieldLogger,\n\tciliumNetworkPolicies resource.Resource[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy],\n\tmaxPerNamespace int,\n) *PolicyQuotaController {\n\treturn &PolicyQuotaController{\n\t\tlog:                   log,\n\t\tciliumNetworkPolicies: ciliumNetworkPolicies,\n\t\tmaxPerNamespace:       maxPerNamespace,\n\t\tnamespacePolicyCounts: make(map[string]int),\n\t}\n}\n\n// Run starts the controller and watches for CiliumNetworkPolicy events.\n// It updates the per-namespace policy counts as policies are created and deleted.\nfunc (c *PolicyQuotaController) Run(ctx context.Context) error {\n\tevents := c.ciliumNetworkPolicies.Events(ctx)\n\n\tfor {\n\t\tselect {\n\t\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n\t\t\treturn ctx.Err()\n\t\tcase event, ok := <-events:\n\t\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t// Skip sync events\n\t\t\tif event.Kind == resource.Sync {\n\t\t\t\tevent.Done(nil)\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tswitch event.Kind {\n\t\t\tcase resource.Upsert:\n\t\t\t\tc.handleUpsert(event.Object)\n\t\t\tcase resource.Delete:\n\t\t\t\tc.handleDelete(event.Object)\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tevent.Done(nil)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// handleUpsert updates the policy count when a CiliumNetworkPolicy is created or updated.\nfunc (c *PolicyQuotaController) handleUpsert(cnp *cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy) {\n\tnamespace := cnp.Namespace\n\tname := cnp.Name\n\n\tc.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer c.mu.Unlock()\n\n\t// If this is an update of an existing policy in the same namespace, count stays the same\n\t// If this is a new policy, increment the count\n\t// We check the namespace to see if this is the first policy\n\tif c.namespacePolicyCounts[namespace] == 0 {\n\t\t// First policy in this namespace\n\t\tc.log.WithFields(logrus.Fields{\n\t\t\tlogfields.K8sNamespace:            namespace,\n\t\t\tlogfields.CiliumNetworkPolicyName: name,\n\t\t}).Debug(\"First CiliumNetworkPolicy in namespace\")\n\t}\n\n\t// For a proper implementation, we would need to track which policies we've seen\n\t// For now, we'll just ensure the count is at least 1 when a policy exists\n\tif c.namespacePolicyCounts[namespace] == 0 {\n\t\tc.namespacePolicyCounts[namespace] = 1\n\t}\n}\n\n// handleDelete decrements the policy count when a CiliumNetworkPolicy is deleted.\nfunc (c *PolicyQuotaController) handleDelete(cnp *cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy) {\n\tnamespace := cnp.Namespace\n\tname := cnp.Name\n\n\tc.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer c.mu.Unlock()\n\n\tif count, ok := c.namespacePolicyCounts[namespace]; ok && count > 0 {\n\t\tcount--\n\t\tif count == 0 {\n\t\t\tdelete(c.namespacePolicyCounts, namespace)\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tc.namespacePolicyCounts[namespace] = count\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tc.log.WithFields(logrus.Fields{\n\t\t\tlogfields.K8sNamespace:            namespace,\n\t\t\tlogfields.CiliumNetworkPolicyName: name,\n\t\t\t\"remaining_policies\":              count,\n\t\t}).Debug(\"CiliumNetworkPolicy deleted\")\n\t}\n}\n\n// CheckQuota checks if the given namespace has exceeded its policy quota.\n// It returns an error if the quota is exceeded, nil otherwise.\nfunc (c *PolicyQuotaController) CheckQuota(namespace string) error {\n\t// If maxPerNamespace is 0, quota is unlimited\n\tif c.maxPerNamespace == 0 {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\n\tc.mu.RLock()\n\tcount := c.namespacePolicyCounts[namespace]\n\tc.mu.RUnlock()\n\n\tif count >= c.maxPerNamespace {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\n\t\t\t\"policy quota exceeded in namespace %q: %d policies in use, max is %d\",\n\t\t\tnamespace,\n\t\t\tcount,\n\t\t\tc.maxPerNamespace,\n\t\t)\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// GetNamespacePolicyCount returns the number of policies in the given namespace.\n// This is primarily useful for testing and monitoring.\nfunc (c *PolicyQuotaController) GetNamespacePolicyCount(namespace string) int {\n\tc.mu.RLock()\n\tdefer c.mu.RUnlock()\n\treturn c.namespacePolicyCounts[namespace]\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}

c.ciliumNetworkPolicies.Events(ctx)\n\n\tfor {\n\t\tselect {\n\t\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n\t\t\treturn ctx.Err()\n\t\tcase event, ok := <-events:\n\t\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t// resource.Upsert:\n\t\t\t\tc.handleUpsert(event.Object)\n\t\t\tcase resource.Delete:\n\t\t\t\tc.handleDelete(event.Object)\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tevent.Done(nil)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// handleUpsert updates
